Railway Maintenance Domain\n\n### 1.1 ECM Framework (EU 2019/779)\n\nThe **Entity in Charge of Maintenance (ECM)** framework establishes legal responsibilities for railway vehicle maintenance. While Dubai Metro is outside EU jurisdiction, the ECM framework represents industry best practice.\n\n#### ECM Function Mapping\n\n| Function | Responsibility | MMS V1.0 Feature | Status |\n|----------|----------------|------------------|--------|\n| **ECM-F1** | Maintenance Management | Dashboard KPIs, compliance tracking | Visualization only |\n| **ECM-F2** | Maintenance Development | Interval definitions, plan visualization | Mock data display |\n| **ECM-F3** | Fleet Maintenance Management | Real-time fleet status, conflict detection | Conflict indicators |\n| **ECM-F4** | Maintenance Delivery | Work order visualization, depot allocation | Visual representation |\n\n#### ECM Compliance Requirements\n\n| Requirement | ECM Article | MMS V1.0 Implementation |\n|-------------|-------------|------------------------|\n| Risk assessment | Art. 5.2 | Conflict detection, overdue warnings |\n| Competence management | Art. 5.3 | Not implemented |\n| Documentation | Art. 5.4 | Not implemented |\n| Performance monitoring | Art. 5.5 | KPI display |\n\n---\n\n### 1.2 RAMS Compliance (EN 50126-1)\n\n**RAMS** = Reliability, Availability, Maintainability, Safety\n\nEN 50126-1:2017 defines the railway RAMS lifecycle. MMS visualizes RAMS metrics.\n\n#### RAMS Metric Definitions\n\n| Aspect | Definition | MMS V1.0 Feature |\n|--------|------------|------------------|\n| **Reliability** | Probability of intended function under stated conditions | MTBF display |\n| **Availability** | Ability to perform required function at given instant | Fleet availability % |\n| **Maintainability** | Probability of maintenance within stated time | MTTR display |\n| **Safety** | Freedom from unacceptable risk | Critical task priority |\n\n#### RAMS Targets\n\n| Metric | Formula | Target | Critical Threshold |\n|--------|---------|--------|-------------------|\n| Fleet Availability | (Fit Trains / Total Trains) x 100 | >= 97% | < 95% |\n| MTBF | Total Operating Hours / Number of Failures | Operator-defined | Operator-defined |\n| MTTR | Total Downtime Hours / Number of Repairs | <= 24 hours | > 48 hours |\n| Schedule Adherence | (On-Time / Scheduled) x 100 | >= 95% | < 90% |\n\n---\n\n### 1.3 EN 15380 Railway Terminology\n\nAll user-facing labels MUST use EN 15380 compliant terminology.\n\n#### Mandatory Term Usage\n\n| EN 15380 Term | Definition | NOT Acceptable |\n|---------------|------------|----------------|\n| Rolling Stock | Railway vehicles requiring maintenance | Vehicle, Asset, Unit |\n| Fleet | Group of rolling stock sharing manufacturer/model | Group, Class, Collection |\n| Depot | Designated maintenance facility | Garage, Workshop, Station |\n| Train Fitness | Binary operational readiness (fit/unfit) | Availability, Health, Status |\n| Run Assignment | Daily allocation of train IDs to routes | Dispatch, Schedule, Trip |\n| Dead Running | Non-revenue movement between locations | Empty movement, Repositioning |\n| Mileage Balancing | Strategy to equalize wear across fleet | Usage balancing |\n\n#### Maintenance Terminology\n\n| Term | Definition | Context |\n|------|------------|---------|\n| PM (Preventive Maintenance) | Scheduled maintenance at defined intervals | Time or mileage-based |\n| CM (Corrective Maintenance) | Unscheduled repair after failure detection | Reactive |\n| CBM (Condition-Based Maintenance) | Triggered by condition monitoring | Sensor-based |\n| Overhaul | Major refurbishment restoring to original condition | Resets counters |\n| Heavy Maintenance | Significant maintenance requiring extended depot stay | Multi-day duration |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Dubai Metro Context\n\n### 2.1 Fleet Composition\n\n| Fleet | Prefix | Count | Line | Depot | Daily Avg km |\n|-------|--------|-------|------|-------|--------------|\n| Alstom | ALT-001 to ALT-079 | 79 | Red Line | Al Rashidiya | 420-475 km/day |\n| Kinki Sharyo | KNK-001 to KNK-049 | 49 | Green Line | Jebel Ali | 400-454 km/day |\n| **Total** | | **128** | | | |\n\n#### Alstom Fleet Characteristics\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| Quantity | 79 trains |\n| Train Designation | ALT-001 through ALT-079 |\n| Cars per Train | 5 |\n| Base Mileage Range | 450,000 - 800,000 km |\n| Assigned Depot | Al Rashidiya |\n\n#### Kinki Sharyo Fleet Characteristics\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| Quantity | 49 trains (newer fleet) |\n| Train Designation | KNK-001 through KNK-049 |\n| Cars per Train | 5 |\n| Base Mileage Range | 320,000 - 600,000 km |\n| Assigned Depot | Jebel Ali |\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 Depot Configuration\n\n| Depot ID | Name | Tracks | Weekly Man-Hours | Serves |\n|----------|------|--------|------------------|--------|\n| depot-red | Al Rashidiya | 5 | 2,800 | Alstom fleet |\n| depot-green | Jebel Ali | 4 | 2,400 | Kinki Sharyo fleet |\n\n#### Combined Resources\n\n| Resource | Value | Calculation |\n|----------|-------|-------------|\n| Total Maintenance Tracks | 9 | 5 + 4 |\n| Weekly Man-Hours | 5,200 | 2,800 + 2,400 |\n| Monthly Man-Hours | 20,800 | 5,200 x 4 weeks |\n| Track Capacity (per day) | 2 trains per track | Industry standard |\n| Daily Maintenance Capacity | 18 trains | 9 tracks x 2 trains |\n\n---\n\n### 2.3 Contract Scope\n\n| Parameter | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| Contract Duration | 12 years |\n| Operator | Keolis MHI |\n| Client | RTA Dubai |\n| Total Rolling Stock | 128 trains |\n| Planning Horizon | 1-12 years |\n| Maintenance Levels | 4 (A/B/C/D checks) |\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data Model\n\n### 3.1 Train Entity\n\n```typescript\n/**\n * Train entity - represents a single rolling stock unit.\n * JSON-serializable for persistence and API transport.\n */\nexport type AssetType = 'ALSTOM' | 'KINKI';\n\nexport interface Train {\n  /** Unique identifier: \"TRAIN-001\" or \"ALT-001\" */\n  id: string;\n\n  /** Human-readable display name */\n  name: string;\n\n  /**\n   * Fleet type for grouping and maintenance profile\n   * ALSTOM: Red Line fleet (79 trains)\n   * KINKI: Green Line fleet (49 trains)\n   */\n  assetType: AssetType;\n}\n\n/** Extended Train with optional fields */\nexport interface TrainExtended extends Train {\n  carsCount?: number;\n  currentMileageKm?: number;\n  avgDailyMileageKm?: number;\n  status?: 'operational' | 'maintenance' | 'out-of-service';\n  depotId?: string;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Task Entity\n\n```typescript\n/**\n * Task types for visual categorization.\n * Maps to color: maintenance=blue, overhaul=orange, inspection=gray\n */\nexport type TaskType = 'maintenance' | 'overhaul' | 'inspection';\n\n/**\n * Maintenance level classification (A/B/C/D check system).\n */\nexport type MaintenanceLevel = 'A' | 'B' | 'C' | 'D';\n\n/**\n * Task entity - represents a scheduled maintenance activity.\n * Dates stored as ISO 8601 strings, NOT Date objects.\n */\nexport interface Task {\n  /** Unique identifier: \"{trainId}-{year}-{index}\" */\n  id: string;\n\n  /** Foreign key reference to Train.id */\n  trainId: string;\n\n  /** Task start date in ISO 8601: \"YYYY-MM-DD\" */\n  startDate: string;\n\n  /** Task end date in ISO 8601: \"YYYY-MM-DD\" */\n  endDate: string;\n\n  /**\n   * Visual category for color coding:\n   * - maintenance: Blue (#1d4ed8)\n   * - overhaul: Orange (#f59e0b)\n   * - inspection: Gray (#6b7280)\n   */\n  type: TaskType;\n\n  /**\n   * Conflict indicator flag.\n   * True if task overlaps another or violates constraints.\n   */\n  hasConflict: boolean;\n\n  /** Optional: ID of task that must complete before this one */\n  predecessorId?: string;\n}\n\n/** Extended Task with optional fields */\nexport interface TaskExtended extends Task {\n  maintenanceLevel?: MaintenanceLevel;\n  manHours?: number;\n  estimatedCost?: number;\n  dependencies?: string[];\n  status?: 'scheduled' | 'in-progress' | 'completed' | 'cancelled';\n  depotId?: string;\n  tracksRequired?: number;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3.3 TaskRender (Computed)\n\n```typescript\n/**\n * Color mapping for task types.\n */\nexport type TaskColor = 'blue' | 'orange' | 'gray';\n\nexport const TYPE_TO_COLOR: Record<TaskType, TaskColor> = {\n  maintenance: 'blue',\n  overhaul: 'orange',\n  inspection: 'gray',\n};\n\n/**\n * TaskRender - computed values for canvas rendering.\n * NEVER persisted - recomputed on data load.\n */\nexport interface TaskRender {\n  id: string;\n  trainIndex: number;     // Y position (0-based index)\n  startDay: number;       // X position (days since start)\n  duration: number;       // Width in days\n  color: TaskColor;       // Derived from type\n  hasConflict: boolean;\n  type: TaskType;\n  predecessorId?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * Transform persistent Task to render-ready TaskRender.\n */\nfunction transformToRender(\n  task: Task,\n  trainIndexMap: Map<string, number>,\n  datasetStartDate: string\n): TaskRender {\n  const trainIndex = trainIndexMap.get(task.trainId);\n  if (trainIndex === undefined) {\n    throw new Error(`Train not found: ${task.trainId}`);\n  }\n\n  const startDay = daysBetween(datasetStartDate, task.startDate);\n  const duration = daysBetween(task.startDate, task.endDate);\n\n  return {\n    id: task.id,\n    trainIndex,\n    startDay,\n    duration,\n    color: TYPE_TO_COLOR[task.type],\n    hasConflict: task.hasConflict,\n    type: task.type,\n    predecessorId: task.predecessorId,\n  };\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3.4 Conflict Representation\n\n#### Conflict Detection Formula\n\n```\nOverlap Conflict:\n  (A.startDay <= B.startDay + B.duration) AND\n  (A.startDay + A.duration >= B.startDay) AND\n  (A.trainId == B.trainId)\n```\n\n#### Conflict Visualization\n\n| LOD Level | Conflict Indicator |\n|-----------|-------------------|\n| MACRO | Red intensity in heatmap cells |\n| MESO | Red background on task block |\n| MICRO | Red border + warning icon on task card |\n\nColor specification: Intent.DANGER red (`#cd4246`)\n\n---\n\n### 3.5 View Configuration\n\n```typescript\n/**\n * Dataset metadata for world bounds calculation.\n */\nexport interface DatasetMeta {\n  startDate: string;    // ISO 8601: \"2024-01-01\"\n  trainCount: number;   // Number of trains\n  years: number;        // Time range in years\n}\n\nexport const DEFAULT_DATASET_META: DatasetMeta = {\n  startDate: '2024-01-01',\n  trainCount: 50,\n  years: 10,\n};\n\n/**\n * Canvas view configuration constants.\n */\nexport interface ViewConfig {\n  pxPerDay: number;        // Pixels per day (X scale)\n  pxPerTrain: number;      // Pixels per train row (Y scale)\n  minZoom: number;         // Minimum zoom level\n  maxZoom: number;         // Maximum zoom level\n  zoomSensitivity: number; // Scroll sensitivity\n  lodThresholds: {\n    macro: number;         // Below this = MACRO\n    micro: number;         // Above this = MICRO\n  };\n}\n\nexport const DEFAULT_VIEW_CONFIG: ViewConfig = {\n  pxPerDay: 10,\n  pxPerTrain: 24,\n  minZoom: 0.1,\n  maxZoom: 5.0,\n  zoomSensitivity: 0.002,\n  lodThresholds: {\n    macro: 0.5,\n    micro: 2.0,\n  },\n};\n\n/** Level of Detail enumeration */\nexport type LODLevel = 'MACRO' | 'MESO' | 'MICRO';\n\n/** Runtime viewport state */\nexport interface ViewportState {\n  zoom: number;    // 0.1 to 5.0\n  panX: number;    // Camera X (world units)\n  panY: number;    // Camera Y (world units)\n  lod: LODLevel;   // Derived from zoom\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Mathematical Formulas\n\n### 4.1 Km Variance (Coefficient of Variation)\n\nPrimary metric for fleet mileage balance. Lower variance = better distribution.\n\n```\nKm Variance % = (Standard Deviation / Mean) * 100\n\nWhere:\n  mean = sum(all train km) / n\n  stddev = sqrt(sum((x_i - mean)^2) / n)\n```\n\n```typescript\nfunction calculateKmVariance(kmValues: number[]): number {\n  if (kmValues.length < 2) return 0;\n\n  const mean = kmValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / kmValues.length;\n  if (mean === 0) return 0;\n\n  const squaredDiffs = kmValues.map(km => Math.pow(km - mean, 2));\n  const variance = squaredDiffs.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / kmValues.length;\n  const stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);\n\n  return (stdDev / mean) * 100;\n}\n```\n\n| Status | Variance | Indicator |\n|--------|----------|-----------|\n| Green (Healthy) | <= 10% | Green badge |\n| Yellow (Warning) | 10% - 15% | Yellow badge |\n| Red (Critical) | > 15% | Red badge |\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Fleet Availability\n\n```\nFleet Availability % = (Fit Trains / Total Trains) * 100\n\nTargets:\n  Target: >= 97%\n  Critical: < 95%\n```\n\n```typescript\nfunction calculateFleetAvailability(fitTrains: number, totalTrains: number): number {\n  if (totalTrains === 0) return 0;\n  return (fitTrains / totalTrains) * 100;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 MTBF / MTTR / MDBF\n\n```\nMTBF = Total Operating Hours / Number of Failures (Hours)\nMDBF = Total Operating km / Number of Failures (Kilometers)\nMTTR = Total Downtime Hours / Number of Repairs (Hours)\n       Target: <= 24 hours, Critical: > 48 hours\n```\n\n```typescript\ninterface FailureMetrics {\n  mtbf: number;\n  mdbf: number;\n  mttr: number;\n}\n\nfunction calculateFailureMetrics(\n  operatingHours: number,\n  operatingKm: number,\n  downtimeHours: number,\n  failureCount: number,\n  repairCount: number\n): FailureMetrics {\n  return {\n    mtbf: failureCount > 0 ? operatingHours / failureCount : Infinity,\n    mdbf: failureCount > 0 ? operatingKm / failureCount : Infinity,\n    mttr: repairCount > 0 ? downtimeHours / repairCount : 0,\n  };\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.4 Coordinate System\n\n#### Constants\n\n| Constant | Value | Description |\n|----------|-------|-------------|\n| `PX_PER_DAY` | 10 pixels | 1 day = 10 pixels on X axis |\n| `PX_PER_TRAIN` | 24 pixels | 1 train row = 24 pixels on Y axis |\n| `minZoom` | 0.1 | Minimum zoom (zoomed out) |\n| `maxZoom` | 5.0 | Maximum zoom (zoomed in) |\n\n#### Coordinate Conversions\n\n```typescript\nconst PX_PER_DAY = 10;\nconst PX_PER_TRAIN = 24;\n\nfunction dayToX(day: number): number {\n  return day * PX_PER_DAY;\n}\n\nfunction trainIndexToY(index: number): number {\n  return -index * PX_PER_TRAIN;\n}\n\nfunction screenToWorld(\n  screenX: number, screenY: number,\n  cameraX: number, cameraY: number,\n  zoom: number,\n  viewportWidth: number, viewportHeight: number\n): { worldX: number; worldY: number } {\n  return {\n    worldX: cameraX + (screenX - viewportWidth / 2) / zoom,\n    worldY: cameraY + (screenY - viewportHeight / 2) / zoom,\n  };\n}\n```\n\n#### LOD Thresholds\n\n| LOD Level | Zoom Range | Time Scale | Rendering |\n|-----------|------------|------------|-----------|\n| MACRO | < 0.5 | 10-20 years | Heatmap (aggregated) |\n| MESO | 0.5 - 2.0 | 2-5 years | Task blocks (instanced) |\n| MICRO | >= 2.0 | 4-8 weeks | Detailed cards (HTML) |\n\n#### Blend Zone\n\n```typescript\nconst BLEND_ZONE_SIZE = 0.15;\n\nfunction calculateOpacity(\n  zoom: number,\n  threshold: number,\n  direction: 'in' | 'out'\n): number {\n  const t = (zoom - threshold) / BLEND_ZONE_SIZE;\n  const clamped = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, t));\n  return direction === 'in' ? clamped : 1 - clamped;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.5 Km Penalty Calculation (Solver)\n\nUsed by allocation solver to prioritize under-utilized trains.\n\n```\ndeviation_pct = |current_km - target_km| / max(target_km, 1) * 100\n\nIf current_km < target_km:\n  penalty = -deviation_pct * 10  (BONUS)\nIf current_km >= target_km:\n  penalty = +deviation_pct * 10  (PENALTY)\n```\n\n```typescript\nfunction calculateKmPenalty(\n  currentKm: number,\n  targetKm: number,\n  fleetAvgKm: number\n): number {\n  const effectiveTarget = targetKm || fleetAvgKm;\n  if (effectiveTarget === 0) return 0;\n\n  const deviationPct = Math.abs(currentKm - effectiveTarget) / effectiveTarget * 100;\n\n  if (currentKm < effectiveTarget) {\n    return -Math.round(deviationPct * 10);\n  } else {\n    return Math.round(deviationPct * 10);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4.6 Haversine Distance (Dead Running)\n\nGreat circle distance between two geographic points.\n\n```\na = sin^2(delta_lat/2) + cos(lat1) * cos(lat2) * sin^2(delta_lon/2)\nc = 2 * atan2(sqrt(a), sqrt(1-a))\ndistance = R * c\n\nWhere: R = 6371 km (Earth's radius)\n```\n\n```typescript\nfunction haversineDistance(\n  lat1: number, lon1: number,\n  lat2: number, lon2: number\n): number {\n  const R = 6371;\n  const toRad = (deg: number) => deg * Math.PI / 180;\n\n  const lat1Rad = toRad(lat1);\n  const lat2Rad = toRad(lat2);\n  const deltaLat = toRad(lat2 - lat1);\n  const deltaLon = toRad(lon2 - lon1);\n\n  const a = Math.sin(deltaLat / 2) ** 2 +\n            Math.cos(lat1Rad) * Math.cos(lat2Rad) *\n            Math.sin(deltaLon / 2) ** 2;\n\n  const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));\n\n  return R * c;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Maintenance Level Mapping\n\n### Authoritative Mapping Table\n\n| Code | Railway Term | Display | Interval (km) | Tolerance | Duration | Man-Hours | Tracks | Cost |\n|------|--------------|---------|---------------|-----------|----------|-----------|--------|------|\n| A | PM1 | A-Check | 10,000 | +/- 2,000 | 4h | 8 | 1 | $2,500 |\n| B | PM2 | B-Check | 50,000 | +/- 5,000 | 16h | 32 | 1 | $8,500 |\n| C | PM3 | C-Check | 200,000 | +/- 20,000 | 72h | 160 | 1 | $45,000 |\n| D | HM | D-Overhaul | 800,000 | +/- 50,000 | 480h | 1,200 | 2 | $180,000 |\n\n#### Terminology Key\n\n| Term | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| **PM1** | Preventive Maintenance Level 1 (Light) |\n| **PM2** | Preventive Maintenance Level 2 (Intermediate) |\n| **PM3** | Preventive Maintenance Level 3 (Scheduled) |\n| **HM** | Heavy Maintenance / Major Overhaul |\n| **OVH** | Full Overhaul / Refurbishment (resets all counters) |\n\n### Maintenance Cascade\n\n```\nFleet Type (e.g., Alstom Red Line)\n |\n +-- Maintenance Profile\n     |\n     +-- PM1 / A-Check (every 10,000 km)\n     |   Duration: 4 hours\n     |\n     +-- PM2 / B-Check (every 50,000 km)\n     |   Duration: 16 hours, INCLUDES PM1 tasks\n     |\n     +-- PM3 / C-Check (every 200,000 km)\n     |   Duration: 72 hours, INCLUDES PM1 + PM2 tasks\n     |\n     +-- HM / D-Overhaul (every 800,000 km)\n         Duration: 480 hours, RESETS counters\n```\n\n### Maintenance Triggers\n\n| Trigger Type | Description | Best For |\n|--------------|-------------|----------|\n| Time-based | Calendar intervals | Simple assets, regulatory |\n| Mileage-based | Odometer intervals (primary) | Wear-dependent components |\n| Condition-based | Sensor thresholds | Critical components |\n| Hybrid | Combined triggers | Most applications |\n\n---\n\n## 6. Domain Rules\n\n### 6.1 Hard Constraints (Never Violate)\n\n| ID | Rule | Rationale |\n|----|------|-----------|\n| HC-1 | Unfit trains NEVER assigned to service | Safety-critical |\n| HC-2 | Maintenance windows are immutable | Planned downtime |\n| HC-3 | Aptitude requirements are binary | Route compatibility |\n| HC-4 | Depot capacity is physical | Track slots |\n| HC-5 | Service cannot be cancelled for balancing | Operations > Optimization |\n\n### 6.2 Soft Constraints (Optimize Within)\n\n| ID | Rule | Weight |\n|----|------|--------|\n| SC-1 | Km balancing priority | 1000 (HIGH) |\n| SC-2 | Dead running minimization | 100 (MEDIUM) |\n| SC-3 | Maintenance depot proximity | 10 (LOW) |\n\n### 6.3 Tolerance Windows\n\n| Level | Tolerance | Overrun Warning | Critical |\n|-------|-----------|-----------------|----------|\n| PM1 / A-Check | +/- 2,000 km | 95% | 105% |\n| PM2 / B-Check | +/- 5,000 km | 95% | 105% |\n| PM3 / C-Check | +/- 20,000 km | 95% | 105% |\n| HM / D-Overhaul | +/- 50,000 km | 95% | 105% |\n\n---\n\n## 7. Train State Machine\n\n```\n    +-----------------------------------------------+\n    |                                               |\n    v                                               |\n+-------+     +------------+     +------------+     |\n|  FIT  |---->| IN-SERVICE |---->| AVAILABLE  |----+\n+---+---+     +------------+     +-----+------+\n    |                                  |\n    |         +------------+           |\n    +-------->|   UNFIT    |<----------+\n              +-----+------+\n                    |\n                    v\n              +------------+\n              |MAINTENANCE |\n              +-----+------+\n                    |\n                    v\n              +------------+\n              |    FIT     |\n              +------------+\n```\n\n| State | Definition | Transitions |\n|-------|------------|-------------|\n| **FIT** | Train operationally ready | IN-SERVICE, UNFIT |\n| **IN-SERVICE** | Running revenue service | AVAILABLE |\n| **AVAILABLE** | Fit but not assigned | IN-SERVICE, UNFIT |\n| **UNFIT** | Requires maintenance | MAINTENANCE |\n| **MAINTENANCE** | Undergoing maintenance | FIT |\n\n---\n\n## 8. Planning Hierarchy\n\n```\n+-------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                MASTER PLAN (Annual/Multi-Year)               |\n|  - Resource allocation across contract period                |\n|  - Major overhaul scheduling (HM/D-Check)                    |\n+-------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                     MONTHLY PLAN                             |\n|  - Medium-scale repairs allocation (PM2/PM3)                 |\n|  - Workload balancing across weeks                           |\n+-------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                      WEEKLY PLAN                             |\n|  - Detailed work orders                                      |\n|  - Staff rostering and track allocation                      |\n+-------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                      DAILY PLAN                              |\n|  - Execution scheduling (PM1/A-Check)                        |\n|  - Real-time adjustments                                     |\n+-------------------------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n### Time Zone Concept (Frozen Periods)\n\n| Horizon | Zone | Constraint | Allowed Changes |\n|---------|------|------------|-----------------|\n| T > 12 weeks | **Liquid** | Soft | Structure, Volume, Frequency |\n| T-12 to T-7 | **Slushy** | Medium | Timing, Resource Allocation |\n| T-7 to T-48h | **Frozen** | Hard | Emergency Only |\n| T < 48h | **Execution** | Fixed | Break-fix only |\n\n### MMS LOD Mapping\n\n| Planning Level | MMS LOD | Zoom Range |\n|----------------|---------|------------|\n| Master Plan | MACRO | < 0.5x |\n| Monthly Plan | MESO | 0.5x - 1.0x |\n| Weekly Plan | MESO | 1.0x - 2.0x |\n| Daily Plan | MICRO | > 2.0x |\n\n---\n\n# PART II: TECHNICAL ARCHITECTURE\n\n## 9. System Overview\n\n### 9.1 Architecture Diagram\n\n```\n+==============================================================================+\n|                          MMS V1.0 GENESIS ARCHITECTURE                        |\n+==============================================================================+\n\n+------------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                              REACT APPLICATION                                |\n|                         (Vite 5.x + React 18.3.1) |\n|-------|------------|---------|---------|\n| **Build Tool** | Vite | 5.x | Fast HMR, ESM-first |\n| **UI Framework** | React | 18.3.1 | Required for BlueprintJS 6 |\n| **UI Components** | BlueprintJS | 6.1.0 | Enterprise UI components |\n| **3D Renderer** | React Three Fiber | 8.17.10 | Declarative Three.js |\n| **3D Helpers** | drei | 9.114.3 | R3F ecosystem |\n| **3D Engine** | Three.js | 0.170.0 | WebGL rendering |\n| **State** | @zazcart/tools | 0.1.0 | Slice-based state machine |\n| **Spatial Index** | RBush | 4.0.1 | R-tree for O(log n) queries |\n| **Immutability** | Immer | 10.2.0 | Reducer state updates |\n\n### 9.3 Magna Rules\n\nThese rules are INVIOLABLE for V1.0:\n\n| Rule | Constraint | Rationale |\n|------|------------|-----------|\n| **MAGNA-001** | React 18.3.1 (NOT 19) | BlueprintJS 6 requires React 18 |\n| **MAGNA-002** | R3F 8.x + drei 9.x | Pairs with React 18 |\n| **MAGNA-003** | 60fps minimum | Demo success criterion |\n| **MAGNA-004** | Desktop-first | Mobile is deferred |\n| **MAGNA-005** | Mock data only | No real mileage integration |\n| **MAGNA-006** | @zazcart/tools for state | Avoid useState stale closures |\n| **MAGNA-007** | RBush for all queries | O(log n) is mandatory |\n\n---\n\n## 10. State Management\n\n### 10.1 Library Overview\n\n**Package:** `@zazcart/tools` (located at `packages/toolkit`)\n\nThe library provides a slice-based state machine pattern with:\n- Immer-powered immutable updates\n- React 18 `useSyncExternalStore` integration\n- Zero-allocation option for 60fps updates\n\n**Note:** `@zazcart/tools` and `@belt/tools` are the SAME library.\n\n### 10.2 createMachine Pattern\n\n```typescript\n// File: apps/canvas/src/state/canvas-machine.ts\nimport { createMachine } from '@zazcart/tools';\nimport { viewportSlice } from './viewport';\nimport { interactionSlice } from './interaction';\n\nexport const canvasMachine = createMachine({\n  id: 'canvas',\n  slices: {\n    viewport: viewportSlice,\n    interaction: interactionSlice,\n  },\n  context: {\n    userID: null,\n  },\n  // CRITICAL: Disable metadata tracking for 60fps\n  metadata: false,\n});\n\nexport const useCanvas = canvasMachine.useMachine;\nexport const useCanvasSelector = canvasMachine.useSelector;\nexport const canvasActions = canvasMachine.actions;\n\nexport const canvasStore = {\n  getState: canvasMachine.getState,\n  dispatch: canvasMachine.dispatch,\n  subscribe: canvasMachine.subscribe,\n};\n```\n\n### 10.3 Slice Definitions\n\n#### Viewport Slice\n\n```typescript\n// File: apps/canvas/src/state/viewport.ts\nimport { createSyncSlice } from '@zazcart/tools';\n\nexport interface CameraPosition {\n  x: number;\n  y: number;\n  zoom: number;\n}\n\nexport interface ViewportSliceState {\n  camera: CameraPosition;\n  canvasSize: { width: number; height: number };\n  isInitialized: boolean;\n  momentum: { velocityX: number; velocityY: number; isActive: boolean };\n  animation: {\n    isAnimating: boolean;\n    startTime: number;\n    duration: number;\n    startX: number; startY: number; startZoom: number;\n    targetX: number; targetY: number; targetZoom: number;\n  };\n  isPanning: boolean;\n  panStart: CameraPosition;\n  cameraPosAtPanStart: CameraPosition;\n}\n\nexport const viewportSlice = createSyncSlice({\n  id: 'viewport',\n  initial: {\n    camera: { x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 },\n    canvasSize: { width: 0, height: 0 },\n    isInitialized: false,\n    momentum: { velocityX: 0, velocityY: 0, isActive: false },\n    animation: {\n      isAnimating: false, startTime: 0, duration: 250,\n      startX: 0, startY: 0, startZoom: 1,\n      targetX: 0, targetY: 0, targetZoom: 1,\n    },\n    isPanning: false,\n    panStart: { x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 },\n    cameraPosAtPanStart: { x: 0, y: 0, zoom: 1 },\n  },\n  cache: { policy: 'session' },\n  reducers: {\n    setCamera(state, payload: CameraPosition) { state.camera = payload; },\n    setZoom(state, payload: number) { state.camera.zoom = payload; },\n    setCanvasSize(state, payload: { width: number; height: number }) {\n      state.canvasSize = payload;\n      state.isInitialized = true;\n    },\n    startPan(state, payload: { x: number; y: number }) {\n      state.isPanning = true;\n      state.panStart = { x: payload.x, y: payload.y, zoom: state.camera.zoom };\n      state.cameraPosAtPanStart = { ...state.camera };\n    },\n    endPan(state) { state.isPanning = false; },\n    startMomentum(state, payload: { velocityX: number; velocityY: number }) {\n      state.momentum = { ...payload, isActive: true };\n    },\n    stopMomentum(state) {\n      state.momentum = { velocityX: 0, velocityY: 0, isActive: false };\n    },\n    reset() { return viewportSlice.initial; },\n  },\n});\n```\n\n#### Interaction Slice\n\n```typescript\n// File: apps/canvas/src/state/interaction.ts\nimport { createSyncSlice } from '@zazcart/tools';\n\nexport interface InteractionSliceState {\n  hoveredTaskId: string | null;\n  selectedTaskId: string | null;\n  focusedTaskId: string | null;\n  mousePosition: { x: number; y: number } | null;\n}\n\nexport const interactionSlice = createSyncSlice({\n  id: 'interaction',\n  initial: {\n    hoveredTaskId: null,\n    selectedTaskId: null,\n    focusedTaskId: null,\n    mousePosition: null,\n  },\n  cache: { policy: 'session' },\n  reducers: {\n    setHoveredTask(state, payload: string | null) { state.hoveredTaskId = payload; },\n    setSelectedTask(state, payload: string | null) { state.selectedTaskId = payload; },\n    setFocusedTask(state, payload: string | null) { state.focusedTaskId = payload; },\n    setMousePosition(state, payload: { x: number; y: number } | null) {\n      state.mousePosition = payload;\n    },\n    clearSelection(state) {\n      state.selectedTaskId = null;\n      state.focusedTaskId = null;\n    },\n  },\n});\n```\n\n### 10.4 Usage Patterns\n\n**Pattern 1: React Component with Selector**\n\n```typescript\nimport { useCanvasSelector, canvasActions, canvasStore } from '../state';\n\nfunction ZoomControls() {\n  const zoom = useCanvasSelector(s => s.viewport.camera.zoom);\n\n  const handleZoomIn = () => {\n    canvasStore.dispatch(canvasActions.viewport.setZoom(zoom * 1.2));\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <button onClick={handleZoomIn}>+</button>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n**Pattern 2: Animation Loop (NO React Hooks)**\n\n```typescript\nimport { useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber';\nimport { canvasStore, canvasActions } from '../state';\n\nfunction CameraAnimator() {\n  useFrame(() => {\n    // CORRECT: Get fresh state every frame\n    const state = canvasStore.getState();\n    const { animation, camera } = state.viewport;\n\n    if (!animation.isAnimating) return;\n\n    const elapsed = Date.now() - animation.startTime;\n    const progress = Math.min(elapsed / animation.duration, 1);\n\n    // Update camera...\n  });\n\n  return null;\n}\n```\n\n**Pattern 3: Event Handler**\n\n```typescript\nconst handleWheel = useCallback((event: WheelEvent) => {\n  event.preventDefault();\n  const state = canvasStore.getState();\n  const { camera } = state.viewport;\n\n  const zoomDelta = -event.deltaY * ZOOM_SENSITIVITY;\n  const newZoom = clamp(camera.zoom * (1 + zoomDelta), MIN_ZOOM, MAX_ZOOM);\n\n  canvasStore.dispatch(canvasActions.viewport.setCamera({\n    x: camera.x, y: camera.y, zoom: newZoom,\n  }));\n}, []);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Canvas Architecture\n\n### 11.1 React Three Fiber Integration\n\n**Version Pairing (Critical):**\n\n| React Version | R3F Version | drei Version |\n|---------------|-------------|--------------|\n| **React 18** | **R3F 8.x** | **drei 9.x** |\n| React 19 | R3F 9.x | drei 10.x |\n\n```typescript\n// Camera configuration\nconst CAMERA_NEAR = -1000;\nconst CAMERA_FAR = 1000;\nconst INITIAL_ZOOM = 1;\n\n<Canvas\n  orthographic\n  camera={{\n    position: [0, 0, 100],\n    zoom: INITIAL_ZOOM,\n    near: CAMERA_NEAR,\n    far: CAMERA_FAR,\n  }}\n  gl={{\n    antialias: true,\n    alpha: false,\n    powerPreference: 'high-performance',\n  }}\n>\n  <CameraController />\n  <LODLayers />\n</Canvas>\n```\n\n### 11.2 Coordinate System\n\n```\n                                    +X (Time - Days)\n                                    |\n        (-) Past                    |                    (+) Future\n   <--------------------------------+--------------------------------->\n                                    |\n                   Day 0 = meta.startDate (2024-01-01)\n\n+Y (Trains - negative because canvas Y grows down)\n|\n|  Train 0:  y = 0\n|  Train 1:  y = -24 (PX_PER_TRAIN)\n|  Train 2:  y = -48\n|  ...\n|  Train 49: y = -1176\nv\n\nConstants:\n  PX_PER_DAY = 10\n  PX_PER_TRAIN = 24\n\nViewport:\n  Camera position (x, y) is CENTER of visible area\n  Visible width = canvasWidth / zoom\n  Visible height = canvasHeight / zoom\n```\n\n---\n\n## 12. LOD System\n\n### 12.1 Three-Layer Architecture\n\n| Layer | Zoom Range | Visualization | Max Instances |\n|-------|------------|---------------|---------------|\n| **MACRO** | < 0.5x | Heatmap cells | 600 |\n| **MESO** | 0.5x - 2.0x | Task blocks | 100,000 |\n| **MICRO** | > 2.0x | HTML labels + curves | 50 labels |\n\n### 12.2 Crossfade Transitions\n\n```typescript\nconst LOD_THRESHOLDS = {\n  macroToMeso: 0.5,\n  mesoToMicro: 2.0,\n};\nconst BLEND_ZONE_SIZE = 0.15;\n\nfunction calculateLayerOpacities(zoom: number): {\n  macro: number; meso: number; micro: number;\n} {\n  const { macroToMeso, mesoToMicro } = LOD_THRESHOLDS;\n\n  const macroEnd = macroToMeso - BLEND_ZONE_SIZE;\n  const mesoStart = macroToMeso + BLEND_ZONE_SIZE;\n  const mesoEnd = mesoToMicro - BLEND_ZONE_SIZE;\n  const microStart = mesoToMicro + BLEND_ZONE_SIZE;\n\n  let macro = 0, meso = 0, micro = 0;\n\n  if (zoom <= macroEnd) macro = 1;\n  else if (zoom < mesoStart) {\n    const t = (zoom - macroEnd) / (mesoStart - macroEnd);\n    macro = 1 - t;\n    meso = t;\n  } else if (zoom <= mesoEnd) {\n    meso = 1;\n  } else if (zoom < microStart) {\n    const t = (zoom - mesoEnd) / (microStart - mesoEnd);\n    meso = 1 - t;\n    micro = t;\n  } else {\n    micro = 1;\n  }\n\n  return { macro, meso, micro };\n}\n```\n\n**Material Configuration:**\n\n```typescript\n<meshBasicMaterial\n  toneMapped={false}\n  transparent={opacity < 1}\n  opacity={opacity}\n  depthWrite={opacity >= 0.5}  // Prevent z-fighting\n/>\n```\n\n### 12.3 Layer Implementations\n\n#### MacroLayer\n\n```typescript\n// InstancedMesh with heatmap coloring\nconst CELL_WIDTH = 30 * 10;  // ~30 days * pxPerDay\nconst CELL_HEIGHT = 24;\n\nexport function MacroLayer({ tasks, trainCount, opacity = 1 }) {\n  const meshRef = useRef<InstancedMesh>(null);\n  const tempObject = useMemo(() => new Object3D(), []);\n  const tempColor = useMemo(() => new Color(), []);\n\n  const totalMonths = 10 * 12;\n  const totalCells = trainCount * totalMonths;\n\n  const densityGrid = useMemo(\n    () => calculateDensityGrid(tasks, trainCount, totalMonths),\n    [tasks, trainCount, totalMonths]\n  );\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!meshRef.current) return;\n    // Update instance matrices and colors based on density...\n  }, [densityGrid]);\n\n  return (\n    <instancedMesh ref={meshRef} args={[undefined, undefined, totalCells]}>\n      <planeGeometry args={[1, 1]} />\n      <meshBasicMaterial toneMapped={false} transparent={opacity < 1}\n        opacity={opacity} depthWrite={opacity >= 0.5} vertexColors />\n    </instancedMesh>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n#### MesoLayer\n\n```typescript\nconst MAX_INSTANCES = 100000;\nconst TASK_HEIGHT = 18;\n\nconst COLORS = {\n  blue: '#3b82f6',\n  orange: '#f59e0b',\n  gray: '#9ca3af',\n};\nconst CONFLICT_COLOR = '#ef4444';\n\nexport function MesoLayer({ tasks, opacity = 1 }) {\n  const meshRef = useRef<InstancedMesh>(null);\n  const tempObject = useMemo(() => new Object3D(), []);\n  const tempColor = useMemo(() => new Color(), []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!meshRef.current) return;\n    meshRef.current.count = tasks.length;\n\n    tasks.forEach((task, i) => {\n      const width = task.duration * PX_PER_DAY;\n      const x = task.startDay * PX_PER_DAY + width / 2;\n      const y = -task.trainIndex * PX_PER_TRAIN - PX_PER_TRAIN / 2;\n\n      tempObject.position.set(x, y, 0);\n      tempObject.scale.set(width, TASK_HEIGHT, 1);\n      tempObject.updateMatrix();\n      meshRef.current.setMatrixAt(i, tempObject.matrix);\n\n      const color = task.hasConflict ? CONFLICT_COLOR : COLORS[task.color];\n      tempColor.set(color);\n      meshRef.current.setColorAt(i, tempColor);\n    });\n\n    meshRef.current.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true;\n    if (meshRef.current.instanceColor) {\n      meshRef.current.instanceColor.needsUpdate = true;\n    }\n  }, [tasks]);\n\n  return (\n    <instancedMesh ref={meshRef} args={[undefined, undefined, MAX_INSTANCES]}>\n      <planeGeometry args={[1, 1]} />\n      <meshBasicMaterial toneMapped={false} transparent={opacity < 1}\n        opacity={opacity} depthWrite={opacity >= 0.5} vertexColors />\n    </instancedMesh>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n#### MicroLayer\n\n```typescript\nconst MAX_VISIBLE_LABELS = 50;\n\nexport function MicroLayer({ tasks, viewportBounds, opacity = 1 }) {\n  const visibleTasks = useMemo(() => {\n    if (!viewportBounds) return tasks.slice(0, MAX_VISIBLE_LABELS);\n    const visible = spatialIndex.queryViewport(viewportBounds);\n    return visible.slice(0, MAX_VISIBLE_LABELS);\n  }, [tasks, viewportBounds]);\n\n  return (\n    <group>\n      <TaskBlocks tasks={tasks} opacity={opacity} />\n      {visibleTasks.map(task => (\n        <TaskLabel key={task.id} task={task} opacity={opacity} />\n      ))}\n      <DependencyLines tasks={visibleTasks} opacity={opacity} />\n    </group>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 13. Performance Architecture\n\n### 13.1 Performance Requirements\n\n| Metric | Target | Confidence |\n|--------|--------|------------|\n| **Frame Rate** | 60fps constant | 70% (desktop) |\n| **Frame Budget** | < 16.67ms | 70% (desktop) |\n| **Viewport Query** | < 1ms | 95% (verified) |\n| **LOD Transition** | < 100ms | 90% |\n| **Memory** | < 100MB stable | 80% |\n\n### 13.2 InstancedMesh Pre-allocation\n\n**Problem:** Dynamic count causes GPU buffer reallocation.\n\n```typescript\n// WRONG: Recreates buffer when length changes\n<instancedMesh args={[geometry, material, tasks.length]}>\n\n// CORRECT: Pre-allocate, control with mesh.count\nconst MAX_INSTANCES = 100000;\n<instancedMesh ref={meshRef} args={[geometry, material, MAX_INSTANCES]}>\n\n// In useEffect:\nmesh.count = actualTaskCount;\n```\n\n**Memory Cost:** 100k instances x 64 bytes = ~6.4MB GPU memory\n\n### 13.3 RBush Spatial Indexing\n\n**MANDATORY: All viewport queries must use RBush. Array.filter() is FORBIDDEN.**\n\n```typescript\nimport RBush from 'rbush';\n\ninterface RBushItem {\n  minX: number; minY: number;\n  maxX: number; maxY: number;\n  id: string;\n}\n\nexport class RBushSpatialIndex {\n  private tree: RBush<RBushItem>;\n  private itemsById: Map<string, RBushItem> = new Map();\n\n  constructor() { this.tree = new RBush(); }\n\n  load(tasks: TaskRender[]): void {\n    this.tree.clear();\n    this.itemsById.clear();\n\n    const items: RBushItem[] = tasks.map(task => ({\n      minX: task.startDay * PX_PER_DAY,\n      maxX: (task.startDay + task.duration) * PX_PER_DAY,\n      minY: -task.trainIndex * PX_PER_TRAIN - PX_PER_TRAIN,\n      maxY: -task.trainIndex * PX_PER_TRAIN,\n      id: task.id,\n    }));\n\n    for (const item of items) {\n      this.itemsById.set(item.id, item);\n    }\n\n    this.tree.load(items);  // Bulk load O(n log n)\n  }\n\n  queryViewport(bounds: ViewportBounds): string[] {\n    const OVERSCAN = 100;\n    const results = this.tree.search({\n      minX: bounds.minX - OVERSCAN,\n      maxX: bounds.maxX + OVERSCAN,\n      minY: bounds.minY - OVERSCAN,\n      maxY: bounds.maxY + OVERSCAN,\n    });\n    return results.map(item => item.id);\n  }\n\n  queryNearest(x: number, y: number, maxDistance = 50): { id: string; distance: number } | null {\n    let radius = 20;\n    let nearest: { id: string; distance: number } | null = null;\n\n    while (radius <= maxDistance) {\n      const candidates = this.tree.search({\n        minX: x - radius, maxX: x + radius,\n        minY: y - radius, maxY: y + radius,\n      });\n\n      for (const item of candidates) {\n        const centerX = (item.minX + item.maxX) / 2;\n        const centerY = (item.minY + item.maxY) / 2;\n        const dist = Math.sqrt((x - centerX) ** 2 + (y - centerY) ** 2);\n\n        if (dist <= maxDistance && (!nearest || dist < nearest.distance)) {\n          nearest = { id: item.id, distance: dist };\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (nearest) return nearest;\n      radius *= 2;\n    }\n\n    return nearest;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 13.4 Object Pooling\n\n**MANDATORY: GC is the primary bottleneck in WebGL applications.**\n\n```typescript\n// In component scope (created once, reused every frame)\nconst tempObject = useMemo(() => new Object3D(), []);\nconst tempColor = useMemo(() => new Color(), []);\nconst tempVector = useMemo(() => new Vector3(), []);\n\n// In animation loop\nuseFrame(() => {\n  // CORRECT: Reuse pooled objects\n  tempVector.set(x, y, z);\n  ref.current.position.copy(tempVector);\n\n  // WRONG: Creates new object every frame\n  // ref.current.position.copy(new Vector3(x, y, z));\n});\n```\n\n### 13.5 GC Avoidance\n\n| Strategy | Implementation | Impact |\n|----------|----------------|--------|\n| Object Pooling | useMemo for temp objects | High |\n| metadata: false | State machine config | Medium |\n| TypedArrays | EntityStore SoA pattern | High |\n| Pre-allocation | InstancedMesh MAX_INSTANCES | High |\n| Bulk operations | RBush.load() | Medium |\n\n**Frame Budget: 16.67ms**\n\n| Operation | Budget | Priority |\n|-----------|--------|----------|\n| GPU Render | ~8ms | Critical |\n| JavaScript | ~5ms | Critical |\n| Layout/Paint | ~2ms | Low |\n| GC | **0ms target** | **Eliminate** |\n\n---\n\n## 14. Data Flow\n\n### Data Generation Pipeline\n\n```\n+-------------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                      DATA GENERATION PIPELINE                      |\n+-------------------------------------------------------------------+\n\n+------------------+     +------------------+     +------------------+\n|   Generator      | --> |   State Store    | --> |   Render Layer   |\n|   (mock-data.ts) |     |   (canvasStore)  |     |   (LOD Layers)   |\n+--------+---------+     +--------+---------+     +--------+---------+\n         |                        |                        |\n         v                        v                        v\n+------------------+     +------------------+     +------------------+\n| Persistent Types |     | Runtime State    |     | GPU Buffers      |\n| - Train          |     | - ViewportState  |     | - InstanceMatrix |\n| - Task           |     | - Interaction    |     | - InstanceColor  |\n| - DatasetMeta    |     | - EntityStore    |     | - HTML overlays  |\n+------------------+     +------------------+     +------------------+\n```\n\n### Viewport Culling Flow\n\n```\n1. User pans/zooms canvas\n        |\n        v\n2. Camera position updates in state\n        |\n        v\n3. Calculate viewport bounds in world coordinates\n        |\n        v\n4. Query RBush spatial index (O(log n + k))\n        |\n        v\n5. Map IDs to TaskRender objects\n        |\n        v\n6. Update InstancedMesh:\n   mesh.count = visibleTasks.length\n   for each task: setMatrixAt, setColorAt\n   mesh.instanceMatrix.needsUpdate = true\n```\n\n---\n\n# PART III: USER EXPERIENCE\n\n## 15. Semantic Zoom Concept\n\n### Core Metaphor\n\n**\"Google Earth for Time\"** - The visualization transforms based on zoom level.\n\n```\n   ZOOM OUT (Macro)              ZOOM LEVEL               ZOOM IN (Micro)\n        <---------------------------------------------------------------->\n\n   +-------------+          +-------------+          +-------------+\n   | ░░▓▓░░░░░░ |          | ▓▓▓ ░░░ ▓▓ |          | +--------+ |\n   | ░░░▓▓▓░░░░ |          | ░░ ▓▓▓ ░░░ |          | | Task A | |\n   | ░▓▓▓░░░░░░ |          | ▓▓ ░░░ ▓▓▓ |          | | 8h     | |\n   +-------------+          +-------------+          +-------------+\n\n   12-YEAR HEATMAP          2-YEAR DNA STRIP        4-WEEK GANTT\n   (Strategic)               (Tactical)              (Operational)\n```\n\n| Zoom Level | Data Representation | User Question |\n|------------|---------------------|---------------|\n| **MACRO** | Aggregated density | \"Where are bottlenecks?\" |\n| **MESO** | Task blocks | \"What's the maintenance rhythm?\" |\n| **MICRO** | Detailed cards | \"What's this week's work?\" |\n\n### Continuous Navigation\n\n| Gesture | Action | Effect |\n|---------|--------|--------|\n| **Drag** | Pan canvas | Navigate through time and trains |\n| **Scroll wheel** | Zoom at cursor | Increase/decrease detail |\n| **Pinch** | Zoom at center | Two-finger zoom |\n| **Double-click** | Zoom in 2x | Quick zoom to point |\n\n---\n\n## 16. Visual Design System\n\n### 16.1 Color Palette\n\n**Primary Colors:**\n\n| Usage | Color | Hex |\n|-------|-------|-----|\n| Background | Zinc 100 | `#F4F4F5` |\n| Surface | White | `#FFFFFF` |\n| Text Primary | Gray 900 | `#111827` |\n| Text Secondary | Gray 500 | `#6B7280` |\n\n**Task Type Colors:**\n\n| Type | Color | Hex |\n|------|-------|-----|\n| Maintenance | Blue 700 | `#1D4ED8` |\n| Overhaul | Amber 500 | `#F59E0B` |\n| Inspection | Gray 500 | `#6B7280` |\n\n**Status Colors:**\n\n| Status | Color | Hex |\n|--------|-------|-----|\n| Conflict | Red 500 | `#EF4444` |\n| Selected | Cyan 500 | `#06B6D4` |\n| Focused | Violet 500 | `#8B5CF6` |\n| Success | Green 500 | `#22C55E` |\n| Warning | Yellow 500 | `#EAB308` |\n\n**Heatmap Gradient:**\n\n```\nLow Density ---------------------------------> High Density\n\n   #FFF3C4      #FDE68A      #FB923C      #EA580C      #DC2626\n   (Yellow)    (Lt Orange)  (Orange)    (Dp Orange)   (Red)\n      |            |            |            |            |\n   0-20%       20-40%       40-60%       60-80%       80-100%\n```\n\n### 16.2 Typography\n\n| Element | Font | Size | Weight |\n|---------|------|------|--------|\n| App Title | System sans-serif | 18px | Bold (700) |\n| Section Headers | System sans-serif | 14px | Semibold (600) |\n| Task Labels | System sans-serif | 11px | Regular (400) |\n| Timeline Dates | System sans-serif | 12px | Semibold (600) |\n| Train IDs | System monospace | 12px | Regular (400) |\n| Tooltips | System sans-serif | 13px | Regular (400) |\n\n---\n\n## 17. |      |\n|          |   +--------+                                       +---+      |\n+----------+---------------------------------------------------------------+\n|                              TIME SCRUBBER                                |\n|  +----------------------------------------------------------------------+|\n|  | [=====================================O=============================] ||\n|  +----------------------------------------------------------------------+|\n+--------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n```\n\n### Component Dimensions\n\n| Component | Width | Height |\n|-----------|-------|--------|\n| Navbar | 100% | 48px |\n| Sidebar | 80px | calc(100vh - 96px) |\n| Timeline | calc(100% - 80px) | 32px |\n| Canvas | calc(100% - 80px) | Remaining |\n| Minimap | 120px | 80px |\n| Zoom Controls | 40px | 80px |\n| Time Scrubber | 100% | 48px |\n\n---\n\n## 18. Interaction Patterns\n\n### 18.1 Pan Navigation\n\n```\nUser drags from A to B\n\n        A ----------------> B\n\nCanvas moves in OPPOSITE direction\n(content appears to move with drag)\n```\n\n**Constraints:**\n- Unconstrained within data bounds\n- Soft-stop at edges with 10% overscan\n- Snap-back animation if dragged beyond\n\n### 18.2 Zoom Interaction\n\n```\nScroll UP (away from user)    ->    Zoom IN (more detail)\nScroll DOWN (toward user)     ->    Zoom OUT (less detail)\n\nZoom anchored at cursor position\n```\n\n**Zoom Range:**\n\n| Constant | Value | Purpose |\n|----------|-------|---------|\n| MIN_ZOOM | 0.1 | 20 years visible |\n| MAX_ZOOM | 5.0 | 1 week visible |\n| DEFAULT_ZOOM | 1.0 | 5 years visible |\n\n### 18.3 Gesture Mapping\n\n| Gesture | Device | Action |\n|---------|--------|--------|\n| Left-drag | Mouse | Pan canvas |\n| Scroll wheel | Mouse | Zoom at cursor |\n| Two-finger scroll | Trackpad | Pan canvas |\n| Pinch | Trackpad/Touch | Zoom at center |\n| Ctrl + Scroll | All | Horizontal pan |\n| Shift + Scroll | All | Vertical pan |\n| Double-click | All | Zoom in 2x |\n\n### 18.4 Momentum Physics\n\n```typescript\nconst FRICTION = 0.93;\nconst MIN_VELOCITY = 0.5;\n\nfunction startMomentum(initialVelocity: { x: number; y: number }) {\n  let velocity = { ...initialVelocity };\n\n  function animate() {\n    velocity.x *= FRICTION;\n    velocity.y *= FRICTION;\n\n    pan(velocity.x, velocity.y);\n\n    const magnitude = Math.sqrt(velocity.x ** 2 + velocity.y ** 2);\n    if (magnitude > MIN_VELOCITY) {\n      requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    }\n  }\n\n  requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 19. Task Interaction States\n\n| State | Visual | Trigger | Exit |\n|-------|--------|---------|------|\n| **Normal** | Base color | Default | Any other state |\n| **Hover** | Brightness +30% | Mouse over | Mouse leave |\n| **Selected** | Cyan border (2px) | Click | Click elsewhere / Escape |\n| **Focused** | Violet ring (3px) | Tab navigation | Tab away |\n| **Conflict** | Red background | hasConflict: true | Data change |\n\n### Selection Flow\n\n```\n         click(task)\n              |\n              v\n       +------------+     click(other) / Escape\n       |  SELECTED  |------------------------+\n       +-----+------+                        |\n             |                               |\n             | click(task)                   |\n             v                               |\n       +------------+                        |\n       |  DETAILS   |------------------------+\n       |   PANEL    |\n       +------------+\n```\n\n---\n\n## 20. Keyboard Navigation\n\n| Key | Action |\n|-----|--------|\n| Tab | Focus next task |\n| Shift + Tab | Focus previous task |\n| Enter / Space | Select focused task |\n| Arrow Up/Down/Left/Right | Pan viewport |\n| +/- | Zoom in/out |\n| Escape | Clear selection / Close panel |\n| Home | Reset view to default |\n| End | Go to end of timeline |\n| Page Up/Down | Jump 1 year back/forward |\n\n---\n\n## 21. {Math.round(zoom * 100)}%\n    </Tag>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### Timeline Header\n\n**Adaptive Label Format:**\n\n| LOD Level | Visible Range | Label Format |\n|-----------|---------------|--------------|\n| MACRO | 10+ years | \"2028\" |\n| MESO | 2-5 years | \"Oct 2028\" |\n| MICRO | 4-8 weeks | \"19 Oct\" |\n\n---\n\n## 23. Appendix B: Glossary\n\n### Railway Domain Terms\n\n| Term | Definition |\n|------|------------|\n| **CBM** | Condition-Based Maintenance |\n| **Dead Running** | Non-revenue movement of rolling stock |\n| **Depot** | Designated maintenance facility |\n| **ECM** | Entity in Charge of Maintenance (EU regulatory framework) |\n| **Fleet** | Group of rolling stock sharing manufacturer/model |\n| **Mileage Balancing** | Strategy to equalize wear across fleet |\n| **RAMS** | Reliability, Availability, Maintainability, Safety |\n| **Rolling Stock** | Railway vehicles requiring maintenance |\n| **Run Assignment** | Daily allocation of train IDs to scheduled services |\n| **Train Fitness** | Binary operational readiness (fit/unfit) |\n\n### Maintenance Terms\n\n| Term | Definition |\n|------|------------|\n| **HM** | Heavy Maintenance |\n| **MDBF** | Mean Distance Between Failures |\n| **MTBF** | Mean Time Between Failures |\n| **MTTR** | Mean Time To Repair |\n| **OVH** | Overhaul (resets counters) |\n| **PM1/PM2/PM3** | Preventive Maintenance levels 1, 2, 3 |\n\n### Technical Terms\n\n| Term | Definition |\n|------|------------|\n| **CP** | Constraint Programming |\n| **LOD** | Level of Detail |\n| **MIP** | Mixed Integer Programming |\n| **SoA** | Structure of Arrays (data layout) |\n\n### MMS-Specific Terms\n\n| Term | Definition |\n|------|------------|\n| **Blend Zone** | Zoom range where two LOD layers crossfade |\n| **DNA Pattern** | Visual pattern of diagonal task stripes |\n| **MACRO Layer** | Heatmap view at zoom < 0.5x |\n| **MESO Layer** | Task block view at zoom 0.5x - 2.0x |\n| **MICRO Layer** | Detailed card view at zoom > 2.0x |\n| **Semantic Zoom** | Google Earth-style LOD switching |\n| **TaskRender** | Computed task data for canvas rendering |\n\n---\n\n## Document History\n\n| Version | Date | Author | Changes |\n|---------|------|--------|---------|\n| 1.0.0 | 2026-01-06 | MMS V1.0 GENESIS | Initial consolidated specification This allows you to create a consistent design system that matches your brand's visual identity.\n\n### Getting Started\n\nTo set up Blueprint, you can install it by running: `npm install @blueprintjs/core @blueprintjs/icons` - this installs the core Blueprint UI Toolkit package as well as the icons package.\n\n---\n\n## Enterprise Design System Best Practices (2025)\n\n### Governance Model\nEstablish a robust governance model to ensure your enterprise design system transcends being merely a collection of components. Integrating rules and governance directly into the design system is crucial.(no content)Governance in design systems refers to a framework for defining roles, responsibilities, and decision-making authority, ensuring a streamlined process. A design system governance framework is key to maintaining the system's effectiveness, ensuring consistency across projects, and aligning with organizational goals.\n\n### Key Benefits\nA design system can streamline workflows by providing a repository of reusable design elements and guidelines, reducing the time and effort required for designing and developing new software features. By minimizing the need for repeated design efforts and extensive quality checks, a design system leads to significant cost savings over time.\n\n### Documentation Requirements\nInclude usage protocols (clear instructions on how to appropriately use design system elements), maintenance procedures (guidelines for regularly updating and maintaining the design system), and issue reporting (a standardized process for users to report problems or suggest improvements).\n\n### 2025 Trends\nThere's a major shift towards a tool-agnostic approach. Services like Specify can give design system teams increased access to design tools and foster greater consistency.(no content)Tools that unify design and development workflows into a single UI will become more prevalent, helping designers to think in terms of components and design systems.\n\n### Cross-Disciplinary Collaboration\nPromoting cross-disciplinary collaboration is a cornerstone in the development and continuous enhancement of a design system. By engaging stakeholders from various disciplines early in the design process, the system becomes more versatile and inclusive, effectively addressing a wider array of needs.\n\n---\n\n## Alternative: Blueprint UI (Web Components)\n\nThere's also a separate project called Blueprint UI (blueprintui.dev) which offers enterprise-grade Web Components that work seamlessly with React, Angular, Vue, or vanilla JavaScript.(no content)It's WCAG 2.1 AA compliant, thoroughly tested, and built for mission-critical applications with full TypeScript support, comprehensive docs, and intuitive APIs.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"50665276-819d-4400-a2ff-2c4024fb31c4","timestamp":"2026-01-09T22:03:42.484Z","toolUseResult":{"query":"BlueprintJS design system guidelines enterprise application best practices 2025","results":[{"tool_use_id":"srvtoolu_011ZuUEvCU3JHtcPdKUB1UNr","content":[{"title":"Blueprint – Documentation","url":"https://blueprintjs.com/docs/"},{"title":"Blueprint JS design system | Figma","url":"https://www.figma.com/community/file/1178851446892338192/blueprint-js-design-system"},{"title":"Blueprint UI","url":"https://blueprintui.dev/"},{"title":"Building Your React Application With Blueprint UI Toolkit -
